Summary							2) Compute wattage of Resistor          Wk = Ek/(0.2*duty cycle)			
 1)  E = Energy 		       Ek (resistor) = Es (shaft pwr) - [ Em (motor) + Ec (amp) ]				     ( Joules)				
										
										
	Step 1)    Compute Rotational Energy of the System, Es (Joules)									
										
	Series (Coe Reference)	Inertia             Mismatch :1                Load to Motor	Motor Rotor Inertia kgm^2	Total Inertia kgm^2	RPM prior to decel	Es (Joules)				
										
										
		#N/A	#N/A	#N/A	#N/A	#N/A				
										
	Step 2)    Calculate the energy lost in the servo motor windings,  Em (Joules)									
										
	Decel. time in Sec	Watts lost per page 5-97 graph	Em (Joules)				Watts Lost:	It will be assumed that in all cases		
								this will be a fixed value based on		
					Decl Time = Accel Time			application torque being equal to motor 		
	#N/A	#N/A	#N/A					rated torque		
										
	Step 3)  Ec value from "Absorbable Servo Amplifier Energy Graph" 									
										
	Joules per page 5-100 (Use 520V worse case)									
			Joules:	It will be assumed that value is 						
				for highest operating voltage.						
										
	#N/A									
										
	Step 4) 	Ek (resistor) = 	 Es (servo system)  - 		 [ Em (motor)	+ Ec (amp)]				
										
		=	#N/A		#N/A	#N/A				
		=	#N/A		 Joules

Regen (3)
Summary							2) Compute wattage of Resistor          Wk = Ek/(0.2*duty cycle)			
 1)  E = Energy 		       Ek (resistor) = Es (shaft pwr) - [ Em (motor) + Ec (amp) ]				     ( Joules)				
										
										
	Step 1)    Compute Rotational Energy of the System, Es (Joules)									
										
	Series (Coe Reference)	Inertia             Mismatch :1                Load to Motor	Motor Rotor Inertia kgm^2	Total Inertia kgm^2	RPM prior to decel	Es (Joules)				
										
										
		#N/A	#N/A	#N/A	#N/A	#N/A				
										
	Step 2)    Calculate the energy lost in the servo motor windings,  Em (Joules)									
										
	Decel. time in Sec	Watts lost per page 5-97 graph	Em (Joules)				Watts Lost:	It will be assumed that in all cases		
								this will be a fixed value based on		
					Decl Time = Accel Time			application torque being equal to motor 		
	#N/A	#N/A	#N/A					rated torque		
										
	Step 3)  Ec value from "Absorbable Servo Amplifier Energy Graph" 									
										
	Joules per page 5-100 (Use 520V worse case)									
			Joules:	It will be assumed that value is 						
				for highest operating voltage.						
										
	#N/A									
										
	Step 4) 	Ek (resistor) = 	 Es (servo system)  - 		 [ Em (motor)	+ Ec (amp)]				
										
		=	#N/A		#N/A	#N/A				
		=	#N/A		 Joules					
										
	Step 5)		Raw Watts to be dissipated = Ek / duty cylce							
	duty cycle (sec)		                     	                   = 	#N/A		Duty Cycle:	From Coe Spreadsheet.		
			    					It is a variable.		
										
	#N/A		 De-rated Watts (Wk) = Ek/0.2*duty cycle							
				                    = 	#N/A

Regen (4)
Summary							2) Compute wattage of Resistor          Wk = Ek/(0.2*duty cycle)			
 1)  E = Energy 		       Ek (resistor) = Es (shaft pwr) - [ Em (motor) + Ec (amp) ]				     ( Joules)				
										
										
	Step 1)    Compute Rotational Energy of the System, Es (Joules)									
										
	Series (Coe Reference)	Inertia             Mismatch :1                Load to Motor	Motor Rotor Inertia kgm^2	Total Inertia kgm^2	RPM prior to decel	Es (Joules)				
										
										
		#N/A	#N/A	#N/A	#N/A	#N/A				
										
	Step 2)    Calculate the energy lost in the servo motor windings,  Em (Joules)									
										
	Decel. time in Sec	Watts lost per page 5-97 graph	Em (Joules)				Watts Lost:	It will be assumed that in all cases		
								this will be a fixed value based on		
					Decl Time = Accel Time			application torque being equal to motor 		
	#N/A	#N/A	#N/A					rated torque		
										
	Step 3)  Ec value from "Absorbable Servo Amplifier Energy Graph" 									
										
	Joules per page 5-100 (Use 520V worse case)									
			Joules:	It will be assumed that value is 						
				for highest operating voltage.						
										
	#N/A									
										
	Step 4) 	Ek (resistor) = 	 Es (servo system)  - 		 [ Em (motor)	+ Ec (amp)]				
										
		=	#N/A		#N/A	#N/A				
		=	#N/A		 Joules					
										
	Step 5)		Raw Watts to be dissipated = Ek / duty cylce							
	duty cycle (sec)		                     	                   = 	#N/A		Duty Cycle:	From Coe Spreadsheet.		
			    					It is a variable.

Regen (5)
Summary							2) Compute wattage of Resistor          Wk = Ek/(0.2*duty cycle)			
 1)  E = Energy 		       Ek (resistor) = Es (shaft pwr) - [ Em (motor) + Ec (amp) ]				     ( Joules)				
										
										
	Step 1)    Compute Rotational Energy of the System, Es (Joules)									
										
	Series (Coe Reference)	Inertia             Mismatch :1                Load to Motor	Motor Rotor Inertia kgm^2	Total Inertia kgm^2	RPM prior to decel	Es (Joules)				
										
										
		#N/A	#N/A	#N/A	#N/A	#N/A				
										
	Step 2)    Calculate the energy lost in the servo motor windings,  Em (Joules)									
										
	Decel. time in Sec	Watts lost per page 5-97 graph	Em (Joules)				Watts Lost:	It will be assumed that in all cases		
								this will be a fixed value based on		
					Decl Time = Accel Time			application torque being equal to motor 		
	#N/A	#N/A	#N/A					rated torque		
										
	Step 3)  Ec value from "Absorbable Servo Amplifier Energy Graph" 									
										
	Joules per page 5-100 (Use 520V worse case)									
			Joules:	It will be assumed that value is 						
				for highest operating voltage.						
										
	#N/A									
										
	Step 4) 	Ek (resistor) = 	 Es (servo system)  - 		 [ Em (motor)	+ Ec (amp)]				
										
		=	#N/A		#N/A	#N/A				
		=	#N/A		 Joules					
										
	Step 5)		Raw Watts to be dissipated = Ek / duty cylce							
	duty cycle (sec)		                     	                   = 	#N/A		Duty Cycle:	From Coe Spreadsheet.		
			    					It is a variable.

Summary							2) Compute wattage of Resistor          Wk = Ek/(0.2*duty cycle)			
 1)  E = Energy 		       Ek (resistor) = Es (shaft pwr) - [ Em (motor) + Ec (amp) ]				     ( Joules)				
										
										
	Step 1)    Compute Rotational Energy of the System, Es (Joules)									
										
	Series (Coe Reference)	Inertia             Mismatch :1                Load to Motor	Motor Rotor Inertia kgm^2	Total Inertia kgm^2	RPM prior to decel	Es (Joules)

	Step 2)    Calculate the energy lost in the servo motor windings,  Em (Joules)									
										
	Decel. time in Sec	Watts lost per page 5-97 graph	Em (Joules)				Watts Lost:	It will be assumed that in all cases		
								this will be a fixed value based on		
					Decl Time = Accel Time			application torque being equal to motor 		
	#N/A	#N/A	#N/A					rated torque

	Joules per page 5-100 (Use 520V worse case)

				for highest operating voltage.						
										
	#N/A									
										
	Step 4) 	Ek (resistor) = 	 Es (servo system)  - 		 [ Em (motor)	+ Ec (amp)]				
										
		=	#N/A		#N/A	#N/A
